# Edge Program ‚ÄĒ Per-Story Prompts (standalone sessions)

**What this is:** one **`‚Ė∂ Story prompt`** per *not-yet-completed* story across every epic, so any Trello card can be pulled and run in a fresh Claude Code session on its own (per the guide ¬ß0.4 convention). Companion to `edge_program_implementation_guide.md` (the stories' full tasks/AC live there) + `edge_program_technical_spec.md` (design) + `sport_data_platform.md`.
**Last updated:** 2026-06-18 _(refresh on any material change)_

**How to use:** copy a story's block into a fresh session. Blocks are **compact by design** ‚ÄĒ they inherit shared context by reference (¬ß = sections of the implementation guide). Every block assumes the **¬ß0.1 conventions**: `dbtf` (not `dbt`); Snowflake via the Snowflake MCP, fully-qualified, no `USE`; never a live Snowflake query on a request path; `uv run python`; hand >1-min scripts to the operator; **do not git commit/push**; market-blind for non-market models (Principle 3); honest-framing for anything user-facing (no win-rate/edge claims). **CI gates BEFORE handoff (never hand off red code): Python ‚Üí `uv run pytest` (Unit Tests CI); dbt ‚Üí `dbtf build --select state:modified+` AND `dbtf compile` (both dbt-Build CI jobs) ‚ÄĒ all green first.** **Every session (model track included) ENDS with an `‚Ź≠ÔłŹ Operator handoff`: the CI-gate result + run-order commands + a copy-pasteable `git add <paths>` of every changed/created file to commit (code, dbt, `sub_model_registry.yaml`, `ablation_results/*.md`, doc edits) + what NOT to commit (artifacts ‚Üí S3/registry) ‚ÄĒ so the repo never drifts out of sync.**

**App stories ‚ÄĒ one fresh session per story:** run app work **one story at a time, each in its own clean session.** For any **[App]** story: open a fresh session, paste the **application-session bootstrap prompt** (persisted at **`app_session_bootstrap.md`**), then paste **exactly one** story block ‚ÄĒ build, then **end with the `‚Ź≠ÔłŹ Operator handoff` checklist** (Lambda rebuild/deploy, dbt commands, scripts to run, the `git add` for files to deploy, changelog line, verify-after-deploy) so the operator knows exactly what to run. Do **not** chain multiple stories through one long-lived session. App surfaces marked **‚Ź≥ ¬ß0.3** are **not hand-authored here** ‚ÄĒ their prompt is *generated by the upstream model session as its final step* (¬ß0.3), filled with the real served PG contract, then run as a normal (bootstrap + that block) app session.

> **ūüö® APP TARGET (every `[App]`/`[App/serving]` block) ‚ÄĒ two live, one dead:** UI ‚Üí **`frontend/` (Next.js) ONLY**; backend/API ‚Üí **`app/backend/` (live FastAPI)**; ‚õĒ **legacy Streamlit UI (`app/streamlit_app.py`, `app/home.py`, `app/pages/`, `app/utils/`) ‚ÄĒ DO NOT EDIT.** Footgun: `app/` is half-alive (`app/backend/` is live; the rest is dead Streamlit), and Next.js has its own `frontend/app/`. First action in any app session: `cat frontend/package.json` to confirm Next.js; if doing UI work and you open `app/home.py` / `app/pages/*.py`, **STOP ‚ÄĒ wrong place.** (Full rule: guide ¬ß0.2.) A prior session edited the Streamlit UI by mistake (2026-06-18) ‚ÄĒ this guard prevents a repeat. **Changelog rule: any change the end user would notice ends with a `frontend/data/changelog.json` entry ‚ÄĒ under the MONDAY of the current week (weeks group Monday‚ÜíMonday; append to that Monday's block, don't key by the literal ship date).**

**Status legend:** ‚¨ú open ¬∑ ūüĒĄ in progress ¬∑ ūüĒí gated ¬∑ ‚úÖ done (no prompt needed).

> **ūüü• ~~Railway MCP~~ ‚ÄĒ OBSOLETE (INC-16, 2026-06-27): we are OFF Railway entirely (plan CANCELLED).** Orchestration is **self-hosted Dagster OSS on AWS EC2** (`i-07594af1679f81c38`); deploys go through the **P5 CD** (merge to `main` ‚Üí OIDC‚ÜíSSM‚Üí`deploy.sh`) or **SSM Session Manager** for a box shell ‚ÄĒ NOT a Railway MCP/dashboard. Serving cache = **DynamoDB `credence-prod-serving-cache`** (no PG, no `DATABASE_URL`). Any "Railway / Railway-cron / Railway-PG" reference in older prompts is STALE.

> **ūüü• DATA SOURCE = S3 LAKEHOUSE (DuckDB), NOT Snowflake ‚ÄĒ applies to EVERY pending story (hardened 2026-06-29).** The E11.1 program has migrated Snowflake ‚Üí S3 parquet (W1‚ÄďW6 done: `mart_pitch_*`, the odds/CLV/team/FanGraphs/posteriors/savant marts, `stg_batter_pitches`, ‚Ä¶ all now S3 parquet; **W7 drops the last Snowflake views + the feature/serving readers ‚Üí end-state Cortex-ONLY**). **So any model/data/feature story reads from the S3 lakehouse via DuckDB ‚ÄĒ NOT Snowflake.** A Snowflake read is now a **RED FLAG** (the object is a thin external-table view today and GONE after W7); the only sanctioned Snowflake use is the Cortex narrative (`generate_pick_narratives.py`). Use the proven lakehouse-read pattern (DuckDB over S3 ‚ÄĒ `run_w1_lakehouse`/`zone_matchup` scripts); assemble the feature matrix ONCE‚Üíparquet for bake-offs (read the cache per candidate, never re-pull). If a source looks Snowflake-only, STOP + flag it as a likely un-migrated straggler (a precursor, not a Snowflake read). **Treat any "query Snowflake / `baseball_data.*` table" instruction in an OLDER prompt below as STALE ‚Üí read the S3 parquet instead.**

## Epic E2 ‚ÄĒ Per-Side Generative Totals  *(market-blind unless noted)*
```

```

‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E2.1-r Per-side count-model BAKE-OFF (revisit of the single-architecture E2.1)   [Model-A ¬∑ market-blind ¬∑ ūüĒ¨ ¬ß0.5 discipline]   (2026-06-24, operator ‚ÄĒ the highest-value model revisit)

**E2.2 ‚ÄĒ ‚úÖ GATE RAN 2026-06-22 ‚ÄĒ honest finding (NOT-MET = the finding, like E2.1b): home/away runs are essentially INDEPENDENT (residual ŌĀ=‚ąí0.0035); the totals variance deficiency is MARGINAL UNDER-DISPERSION, not dependence.** Harness: `betting_ml/utils/copula.py` (discrete distributional-transform ‚Üí normal-scores ŌĀ estimator, `kendall_tau_to_rho`, vectorized `sample_gaussian_copula_negbin`, `analytic_total_variance`, `GaussianCopulaParams`) + `betting_ml/scripts/totals_generative/fit_copula.py` (OOS-purged-CV marginals, ŌĀ + ŌĀ/r bucket-conditioning, sim+analytic AC validation, **dispersion diagnostic**) + 14 tests `betting_ml/tests/test_copula.py`; `uv run pytest` 405‚úď/1s. **Operator run (11,659 eval games 2021‚Äď25):** residual ŌĀ=‚ąí0.0035 (Kendall ‚ąí0.0046, naive raw +0.0002) ‚Üí **copula UNNECESSARY** (global, no material bucket ŌĀ); corr AC ‚úÖ, but **var(total) AC ‚ĚĆ ‚ÄĒ copula 15.15 ‚Čą independent 15.18 vs empirical 19.99 (~24% shortfall, identical with/without coupling)** ‚áí the gap is in the MARGINALS. **Root cause = under-dispersion: E2.1 fits NegBin `r` on optimistic TRAIN-fit means ‚Üí `r` too high; the dispersion diagnostic confirms an OOS-calibrated `r` (~4 vs train ~6‚Äď15) reproduces var(total) ‚Üí closes the gap.** **ūüĒĎ Load-bearing design choice (still correct):** ŌĀ was fit on the RESIDUAL dependence after E2.1 conditional means absorb shared park/weather/ump (distributional-transform‚Üínormal-scores), NOT raw pairs (double-count). **‚ě°ÔłŹ E2.3 directives: (1) DROP the copula coupling (ŌĀ‚Čą0, convolve independently); (2) CALIBRATE the per-side dispersion on HELD-OUT residuals, not E2.1's train-fit r ‚ÄĒ that is the lever for calib_80‚Č•0.80 / PIT.** Operator: re-run `fit_copula.py` once to bake the dispersion diagnostic into `ablation_results/e2_2_copula_fit.json` + `e2_2_copula_decision.md` (first run predated that block). `copula_v1.json` records ŌĀ_global‚Čą0.

**E2.3 ‚ÄĒ ‚úÖ PRODUCT-COMPLETE 2026-06-24 (operator gate + per-side re-run, 11,662 eval games 2021‚Äď25): total + team-totals CALIBRATED; run-diff = documented accepted near-miss ‚Üí proceed to E2.5.** `betting_ml/utils/totals_distribution.py` (pure, unit-tested: leakage-safe dispersion MLE + expanding-window `calibrate_dispersion_expanding`, independent convolution `draw_independent_samples` via the E2.2 sampler at ŌĀ=0 with per-side `r_home`/`r_away`, total/run-diff/team-total derivation, P05‚Ä¶P95 `quantile_grid` + `prob_over`, randomised-PIT + `interval_coverage`, `TotalsDistributionParams`) + `betting_ml/scripts/totals_generative/fit_totals_distribution.py` + `betting_ml/tests/test_totals_distribution.py` (17 tests). **GATE RESULT:** dispersion thesis VALIDATED ‚ÄĒ leakage-safe expanding held-out `r` stable per-side (**r_home 4.03 / CV 0.008, r_away 3.57 / CV 0.023**; fixes E2.1's under-dispersed 8.5). **Total ‚úÖ (calib_80 0.838, PIT-flat 0.0068); team-totals ‚úÖ (home 0.863, away 0.847)** ‚Üí core totals deliverable MET + serving-ready (`totals_distribution_v1.json`). **run_diff = ACCEPTED near-miss** on PIT-flatness (0.0303 vs 0.025; coverage 0.839 + center 0.503 fine). **Cause SETTLED, 2 lines:** (1) synthetic ‚ÄĒ correct model gives FLAT run_diff (0.0067), dispersion-asymmetry alone caps ~0.015; (2) the per-side re-run MOVED home/away dispersion (r_home 4.03 > r_away 3.57) but left run_diff UNCHANGED (0.0301‚Üí0.0303) ‚áí the miss is NOT dispersion but the tiny home/away DEPENDENCE the independent convolution omits BY DESIGN (E2.2 ŌĀ‚Čą0: negligible for the *total* which passes, but the *difference* is uniquely sensitive). **NOT chased:** the only fix = re-add a copula (contradicts E2.2 ‚ÄĒ don't force a coupling the data lacks) and run_diff is NOT a served surface (shipped H2H uses the calibrated E13.6 model). ‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E5.2 Per-prop distributional pricing ‚ÄĒ ‚≠ź LEAD = PITCHER STRIKEOUTS (the synthesis bet)   [Model-A ¬∑ market-blind pricing; edge gate = E5.3 ‚Üí E5.4]   (enriched 2026-06-24)

DO ‚ÄĒ price each prop from the player's predictive distribution. **For pitcher_strikeouts specifically, model K = K-RATE √ó BATTERS-FACED**, each component explicitly:
 (1) **K-RATE** ‚ÄĒ NegBin/Poisson per-PA K rate with **EB CAREER + LEAGUE priors** (the small-sample shrinkage edge: early-season / post-return, shrink the raw rate toward career/league and let data take over as n grows). Condition on platoon split (vs LHB/RHB), pitch-arsenal composition, and ‚≠ź **CATCHER FRAMING** ‚ÄĒ the underweighted factor (borderline strike‚ÜíK; we have the data, books rarely price it). **‚ö†ÔłŹ TEMPER per E13.2 (2026-06-24): for PA outcomes, platoon/TTO added ‚Čą0 CONDITIONAL on batter√ópitcher identity (the signal is ~all identity, which log5 + any decent K model already capture). So do NOT lean the K edge on platoon/matchup conditioning ‚ÄĒ lean it on (a) the genuinely-underweighted CATCHER FRAMING, (b) the small-sample EB-shrinkage advantage early-season/post-return, and (c) the MARKET being lazy (the bet is the BOOK misprices K lines off recent-avg+reputation, NOT that we have a better matchup model). If the K-prop market turns out as efficient as the game-level ones, expect a clean null at E5.4 ‚ÄĒ and that's fine.**
 (2) **BATTERS-FACED ‚ÄĒ the K-opportunity DENOMINATOR via a SURVIVAL/hazard model of pitcher workload**: P(reach F5) / expected batters faced as a hazard on pitch-count + velocity-decay + run-environment + manager-pull tendency (we have the pitch-level velocity). This answers "how many ABs does this SP actually get," which the K count depends on.
 (3) **F5 SCOPING** ‚ÄĒ also price the FIRST-5-INNINGS K window (rides the E5.1 F5 backfill): removes bullpen noise, isolates the starter = the cleanest scope.
 Convolve (1)√ó(2) ‚Üí the K-count predictive distribution ‚Üí P(over/under) at the book's line. Also price the other phase-1 props (pitcher_outs from starter_ip_v1 directly; batter_total_bases/hits from the per-batter PA distribution), but pitcher_strikeouts is the LEAD.
Gate/AC: per-prop P(over/under) at the line; PIT-calibrated + per-prop reliability/ECE under E1.1 CV. ‚áí feeds E5.3 (edge/de-vig vs the K line) ‚Üí **E5.4 (the HARD gate ‚ÄĒ the crux: calib_80, PBO<0.2/DSR>0 per market multiple-comparison-corrected, forward CLV NET OF the high prop vig)**. HONEST: calibration ‚Č† edge ‚ÄĒ a well-calibrated K distribution is product value (projections) even if E5.4 returns null. ‚ö†ÔłŹ Needs the E5.1 K-prop backfill (in progress).
```
```
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E5.3 Edge, de-vig & per-book comparison ‚ÄĒ pitcher strikeout props   ‚úÖ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-25. Built `betting_ml/utils/prop_edge.py` (pure, 24 tests: two-way de-vig + hold, half/integer-line PUSH, EV-with-refund, name normalisation) + `betting_ml/scripts/prop_pricing/edge_devig_props.py` (scores the served `strikeout_glm_v1.pkl` distribution off the cached frame ‚ÄĒ NO Snowflake; S3-first DuckDB line read). **NAME‚ÜíID BRIDGE SOLVED:** `ref_players` first/last ‚Üí "First Last" ‚Üí `normalize_name` (accents/punct/Jr.‚ÄďSr.) + a **(last-name, first-initial) fallback** (feed full-legal-names "Matthew Boyd" ‚ÜĒ ref "Matt Boyd") + a **¬Ī1-day UTC window** (S3 `commence_time` UTC vs local prediction date ‚ÄĒ the big resolver). **JOIN COVERAGE 7,351/7,774 = 94.6%** (full-name 7,073 + last-initial 278; rest FLAGGED: 302 no-start/scratch/IL/cold-start, 112 not-a-modelled-starter, 9 ambiguous). 63,765 (pitcher√ódate√óbook√óline) rows, 14 books; Pinnacle anchors 81.3% (NOT thin). ‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E5.3 Edge, de-vig & per-book comparison ‚ÄĒ pitcher strikeout props   [Model-B ¬∑ market-AWARE (de-vig); feeds E5.4]   (fleshed 2026-06-25)
WHY: E5.2 shipped the served market-blind K distribution (`poisson_glm_k`). E5.3 is the FIRST market-aware step: de-vig each book's K over/under line, compare the model's P(over/under) at that line vs each book's de-vigged implied, and emit a per-(pitcher √ó date √ó book √ó line) **edge + EV table** with Pinnacle as the sharp fair-value anchor where it prices K props. **This is NOT an edge claim** (best_alpha=0) ‚ÄĒ it's the model-vs-market comparison table that E5.4 then GATES for cashability. Market data is allowed here (it's a de-vig step, not a market-blind model).
ūüĒĎ THE E5.2-FLAGGED BLOCKER ‚ÄĒ NAME‚ÜíID BRIDGE: the E5.1 S3 K-prop lines key on `player_name` (NO player_id); the E5.2 predictions key on `pitcher_id`. **Wire the `ref_players` name‚Üípitcher_id bridge to join them** ‚ÄĒ handle ambiguity (duplicate names, accents, Jr./Sr., nicknames). A JOIN-COVERAGE report (how many of the ~7,774 player√ódate closing lines resolve to a prediction) is part of the deliverable; flag unresolved names, don't silently drop them.
ūüíĺ DATA (per ¬ß0.5): the E5.1 K closing lines are in S3 (~7,774 player√ódate √ó book) ‚ÄĒ read via DuckDB, NOT a fresh Snowflake pull. Predictions come from the E5.2 served bundle `strikeout_glm_v1.pkl` (gitignored ‚Üí regenerate via the E5.2 STEP-2 command if absent).
Read: ¬ß5B E5.3 + ¬ß0 + master A0.4.32 (the per-book de-vig + comparison pattern for GAME markets ‚ÄĒ extend it to props) + `betting_ml/utils` devig_* (reuse ‚ÄĒ two-way de-vig) + the E5.2 `prop_pricing.py` + `strikeout_glm_v1.pkl` (the served K distribution + its API) + the E5.1 S3 K-line layout + `ref_players`.
DO:
 ‚ÄĘ JOIN: load the E5.2 K predictive distribution per (pitcher_id, date) ‚Üí join to the S3 K lines via the `ref_players` bridge ‚Üí one row per (pitcher, date, book, K-line).
 ‚ÄĘ DE-VIG each book's two-way K price (over/under) ‚Üí the book's de-vigged implied P(over) (reuse devig_*; two-sided at the line).
 ‚ÄĘ MODEL P at the book's EXACT line off the E5.2 distribution ‚ÄĒ P(K > line) for a half-line (e.g. 5.5), and handle the integer-line PUSH convention explicitly (e.g. line 6 ‚Üí over = P(K‚Č•7), push = P(K=6)); don't fudge the half vs integer.
 ‚ÄĘ EDGE = model P ‚ąí book de-vigged P; EV per $1 at the book's offered price. Per book + a Pinnacle sharp-anchor column WHERE Pinnacle prices K props (‚ö†ÔłŹ Pinnacle prop coverage may be thin ‚Üí flag, don't assume).
 ‚ÄĘ OUTPUT: the per-(pitcher √ó date √ó book √ó line) prop edge/EV table + the join-coverage report ‚Üí `ablation_results/e5_3_*` (and the shape E5.4 will read).
ūüĒí HONEST FRAMING (required): a transparency / model-vs-market comparison, NOT a bet rec. The prop VIG is LARGE ‚Üí net-of-vig is the only honest read; "edge" here is model-relative and UNPROVEN until E5.4. No +EV claim.
Gate/AC: per-(pitcher√ódate√óbook√óline) edge + EV table; per-book de-vig correct (two-way; integer-line push handled); name‚Üíid join-coverage report with unresolved flagged; Pinnacle anchor where available; honest framing; `uv run pytest -m "not slow"` green. Feeds E5.4.
Closeout (per ¬ß0.1): END with an ‚Ź≠ÔłŹ Operator handoff ‚ÄĒ run-order + `git add` (the E5.3 module + table records + any ref-bridge code) + the join-coverage number + where the edge table lands.
```
```
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E5.4 Validation gates ‚ÄĒ the HARD prop-edge gate (the crux: props overfit easily)   [Model-A ¬∑ cashability decision ¬∑ needs E5.3 + E1.4]   (fleshed 2026-06-25)
WHY: E5.3 produces the per-book prop edge table; E5.4 DECIDES whether any of it is a REAL, cashable edge or a clean null. **This is THE gate** ‚ÄĒ props are the easiest place to overfit (many prop types √ó players √ó lines √ó books = a huge multiple-comparison surface), so the discipline here is non-negotiable. A calibrated K distribution (E5.2) is product value; whether it's PROFITABLE is decided ONLY here.
ūüĒí THE GATE (ALL required, ALL pre-registered BEFORE looking at outcomes):
 1. **CALIBRATION FLOOR** ‚ÄĒ calib_80 ‚Č• 0.80 per prop type under E1.1 purged walk-forward CV (E5.2 met this for K = 0.8104; re-confirm on the served glm + extend to any other prop type tested).
 2. **PBO < 0.2 AND DSR > 0 PER MARKET, multiple-comparison-corrected ACROSS EVERY prop-type √ó line √ó book tried** ‚ÄĒ DSR deflates for the number of configs, so **LOG EVERY combination tested** and feed the full count into the deflation. No cherry-picking the best-looking market.
 3. **POSITIVE FORWARD CLV NET OF THE (HIGH) PROP VIG vs the prop's OWN close** ‚ÄĒ the cashability gate. Offline edge is necessary-NOT-sufficient; the verdict is forward CLV on the actual prop closes, net of the large prop vig (gross "edge" that the vig eats is not edge).
 4. **COVERAGE/ROBUSTNESS report** ‚ÄĒ per-market sample sizes, edge distribution, sensitivity to the line/book set.
‚ö†ÔłŹ THE TRAP (non-negotiable ‚ÄĒ the prop data-mining machine): "find the markets/lines where we'd have won" manufactures fake edges. The market/line/book SELECTION is PART of the test ‚Üí pre-register the markets to test, select/fit IN-FOLD (never on the eval fold), count every config in the DSR deflation, judge on held-out/FORWARD CLV. A market that looks +EV in-sample but fails the deflated gate is REJECTED. (Same discipline as E13.9/E13.13.)
ūüĒ≠ MEASUREMENT: forward CLV needs prop CLOSES going forward. E5.1 has the HISTORICAL closes (use them for the backtest leg); LIVE forward prop capture is an E5.0/E5.5-class enrichment not yet built ‚Üí stand up forward accrual via the E13.5-style shadow harness, OR run the historical-close backtest now + flag that the FORWARD leg accrues live before any ship. Offline backtest = necessary; forward = the real verdict.
ūüíĺ DATA (per ¬ß0.5): reads the E5.3 edge table + the E5.1 S3 closes ‚ÄĒ S3/cached, NO fresh Snowflake pull.
Read: ¬ß5B E5.4 + ¬ß0 + ¬ß5 gates + E1.4 (the PBO/CSCV + DSR implementations) + E5.3 (the edge table this gates) + the E13.13 derivative-gate pattern (same forward-CLV-net-of-vig discipline) + `betting_ml` eval (purged CV / PBO / DSR / forward CLV).
DO: implement the gate over the E5.3 table; pre-register the prop markets/lines tested (write them down first); run purged-CV calib + PBO/DSR per market (multiple-comparison-corrected) + forward CLV net of vig vs the prop's own close; produce a clear SHIP/NULL verdict + a dossier (`ablation_results/e5_4_*`). IF a market clears ‚Üí it's the program's FIRST real betting edge ‚Üí flag for serving (the E5.5 prop app surface + the E10.2 uncertainty-aware sizing). IF null ‚Üí dossier entry + close the K-prop hypothesis honestly.
HONEST EXPECTATION: **likely NULL** ‚ÄĒ H2H dead √ó5, main total ~coinflip, E13.8 confirms market efficiency. A clean leak-tight null here is a PLAUSIBLE, ACCEPTABLE outcome (it completes the dossier + closes the K-prop hypothesis with integrity). A survivor = the FIRST real edge. **Do NOT let E5.2's "well-calibrated" get reframed as "profitable" ‚ÄĒ that's decided HERE, only.**
Gate/AC: per-market calib_80 ‚Č• 0.80 + PBO<0.2 + DSR>0 (multiple-comparison-corrected) + forward CLV net of vig; EVERY tested config logged (no cherry-pick); a clear ship/null verdict + dossier; honest framing; `uv run pytest -m "not slow"` green.
Closeout (per ¬ß0.1): END with an ‚Ź≠ÔłŹ Operator handoff ‚ÄĒ run-order (long CV/forward fits ‚Üí operator, >1-min flagged) + `git add` (the gate code + `ablation_results/e5_4_*`) + the verdict + (if ship) the E5.5/serving + E10.2-sizing fast-follow; (if null) the dossier line closing the hypothesis.
```

```

E5.6 = the PROPS-CONSUMER application of that signal (feed the zone-matchup feature into the E5.2 K/prop pricing once E13.10 produces it). Build E13.10 once; E5.6 just consumes it. ```
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E5.7 NLP injury/role/availability signal (props enrichment)   [Model ¬∑ research ¬∑ ūüĒģ FUTURE ‚ÄĒ gated on E5.2 showing promise; heavier/different-competency]   (2026-06-24, synthesis)
WHY: unstructured real-time info (beat-reporter language, manager pressers, team notes) isn't in Statcast until AFTER the market prices it. Hedged/graded language ‚ÄĒ "working through discomfort," "day-to-day," "on a pitch count," "stretched out after a short outing" ‚ÄĒ is processed inconsistently by books + the public. Parsing it ‚Üí a P(availability) / expected-IP adjustment lets us move the K-prop posterior BEFORE the line moves (the information-timing edge). It's the most novel signal source on the synthesis list AND it amplifies E5.2 K props specifically (pitch-count/role language ‚Üí batters-faced ‚Üí K opportunity).
ūüĒí GATE: pursue ONLY after E5.2 shows promise at E5.4 ‚ÄĒ don't build a heavy NLP pipeline to enrich a market that hasn't cleared the gate. Different-competency build + the friction is data LABELING (not modeling) ‚Üí a follow-on, not a now-build, not parallel.
DO (when greenlit): a fine-tuned small transformer (DistilBERT-class) on a domain-labeled set ‚Üí map injury/role language ‚Üí P(availability) + an expected-IP/batters-faced delta, feeding the E5.2 K posterior + the survival denominator. Plus a "market-sentiment-vs-line-divergence" flag (public narrative bullish on a pitcher but our model isn't ‚Üí a higher-confidence fade). Input: a beat-reporter RSS / X feed. Held to the same forward-CLV gate as everything else.
```
```
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E10.2 Uncertainty-aware (posterior) bet sizing   [Model/serving ¬∑ staking-layer correctness ¬∑ closed-form NOT RL ¬∑ gated on a PROVEN edge]   (2026-06-24, synthesis)
WHY: standard fractional Kelly assumes the edge is a point estimate. Our Bayesian models produce a POSTERIOR over edge ‚Üí Kelly on the posterior MEAN systematically OVERBETS because it ignores the variance in the edge estimate itself (the same Jensen's-inequality error that helped kill the totals model). We already SHOW the credible interval on every pick ‚ÄĒ we should SIZE by it too (on-brand: honest uncertainty ‚Üí honest stake).
DO (closed-form, NOT RL): stake by integrating expected log-growth over the edge POSTERIOR (or the simpler equivalent: fractional Kelly shrunk by the posterior-CI width) so a wide-CI edge is staked smaller than a tight-CI edge of the same mean. + a cheap CORRELATION DISCOUNT for simultaneous bets sharing systematic risk (same pitching staff / weather / park) so correlated losses don't compound drawdown. Explicitly NOT the RL framing ‚ÄĒ over-engineering for the core win (revisit RL portfolio optimization only if multi-game effects ever become material; filed, not built).
ūüĒí GATE/SEQUENCING: this only matters once there's a PROVEN edge to size (E5.2 K props or an E13.13 derivative clearing the CLV gate). Don't build speculatively before an edge exists ‚ÄĒ but it's the correct sizing layer the moment one does. Cheap. HONEST: it's bet-SIZING correctness (protects the bankroll from the overbet), NOT an edge source.
```
```
‚Ė∂ ūüóāÔłŹ FILED SYNTHESIS IDEAS (2026-06-24) ‚ÄĒ right-tool-wrong-time / hygiene; NOT scoped as stories (revisit if conditions change):
- Kalman filter for time-varying team strength ‚Üí a lighter closed-form alternative to the Sequential Prior Update Engine; a COMPUTE/COST optimization for the SPUE if its update lag ever bites. File, don't build.
- Multi-armed bandits (Thompson Sampling) for market allocation ‚Üí the Bayesian-natural way to allocate attention ACROSS markets ‚ÄĒ but only once we have ‚Č•2 PROVEN markets (K props + a derivative). Zero proven markets today. Revisit then.
- Causal inference / DAGs / do-calculus for feature validation ‚Üí our leak-clean + purged-CV + orthogonality discipline already catches the worst confounding (the de-leak was a causal-validity catch). Full machinery = over-engineering for the marginal gain. Low-pri hygiene.
- Line-movement TIMING (bet-now-vs-wait) ‚Üí needs tick-level odds we don't have (paid; not after a credit crunch). Defer.
- Calibration methodology (ECE/reliability/isotonic) ‚Üí NOT a gap ‚ÄĒ it's a core STRENGTH (E13.6, the v6 recalibration, E13.2 ECE 0.0026); already a standing pre-deploy gate. Just apply it to the K model.
Gate/AC: explicit Phase-1 kill/proceed verdict; Phase-2 promote accuracy-first only; viz shipped; NOT in the pre-lineup path.
```

(This expansion is REQUIRED for honesty: without netting out deposits/withdrawals, a deposit reads as "growth" ‚ÄĒ misleading. So per-book cash-flow tracking is the only way the growth % is truthful.)
DEP: E9.10 shipped `/users/profile` + the editable `initial_deposit` (DynamoDB users) ‚ÄĒ that single field GENERALIZES here (migrate it as the seed deposit on a default book). Cross-ref E9.16 Bet Log.

Add the bankroll fields ALONGSIDE `portfolio` ‚ÄĒ do NOT overwrite the user item / clobber that attribute (use attribute-level updates, not a full `put_item` that drops other fields). The Lambda already has this table's grant. NOTE: this is a backend/Lambda change ‚ÄĒ decoupled from the INC-16 EC2 box (orchestration), so it's safe to ship during the soak; just keep its commit separate from any INC-16 work.
Read: ¬ß5F E9.17 + ¬ß0.2 + E9.10 (the existing profile field + `/users/profile` endpoint + `services/dynamo.py`) + the Performance page (where growth shows) + the curated book set (BetMGM/Caesars/FanDuel/DraftKings/Fanatics/Bovada/Pinnacle ‚ÄĒ reuse the same names as Book Comparison).
DO:
 ‚ÄĘ DATA MODEL (DynamoDB): per-user, a set of BOOK ACCOUNTS ‚ÄĒ `{book, current_balance}` (user-editable) ‚ÄĒ plus a BANKROLL-EVENT log ‚ÄĒ `[{book, type: deposit|withdrawal, amount, date}]` (a `bankroll_events` list on the user record, or a small `credence-prod-user-bankroll-events` table keyed by Cognito `sub`). Migrate the legacy `initial_deposit` ‚Üí a seed `deposit` event on a default/"unspecified" book.
 ‚ÄĘ BACKEND: extend `/users/profile` or add `/users/bankroll` endpoints ‚ÄĒ GET (books + balances + events + computed growth), PUT (edit a book's current balance; add/rename/remove a book), POST (record a deposit or withdrawal event {book, type, amount, date}). Validate amounts ‚Č• 0; idempotent-safe.
 ‚ÄĘ THE HONEST GROWTH MATH (the crux): per book AND overall ‚ÄĒ `net_deposits = ő£ deposits ‚ąí ő£ withdrawals`; **betting P&L = current_balance ‚ąí net_deposits**; **growth % = betting P&L / ő£ deposits** (cost basis). **A deposit is NOT growth; a withdrawal is NOT a loss** ‚ÄĒ both are cash transfers netted out so the % reflects betting performance. **On the "withdrawal resets tracking" intuition: by default it does NOT reset ‚ÄĒ it's netted into the cash-flow baseline so the metric stays honest.** Offer an explicit, opt-in "reset baseline" action per book if the user truly wants a fresh start (clearly labeled; not the default).
 ‚ÄĘ FRONTEND: Settings ‚Üí "Sportsbooks" ‚ÄĒ list each book with its editable current balance + an "Add deposit / Record withdrawal" control (amount + date) + an event history; "Add a sportsbook" to track more than one. Performance ‚Üí OVERALL growth % + net P&L + net deposits, and a per-book breakdown; keep it LABELED DISTINCTLY from ROI (ROI = return on stake/turnover; growth = return on deposited bankroll ‚ÄĒ do NOT relabel ROI). Hide growth until at least one book + deposit is set.
 ‚ÄĘ This is a MANUAL bookkeeping ledger (user-entered balances/cash-flows) ‚ÄĒ do NOT try to auto-derive balances from settled bets (that's a different, larger feature; the Bet Log E9.16 is separate). Self-reported.
HONEST FRAMING: it's the USER's own tracked bankroll across their books ‚ÄĒ not a model edge claim; the growth % nets out cash flows so it's an honest betting-results figure, not inflated by deposits.
Gate/AC: per-book editable balances; deposit + withdrawal events recorded with date; overall + per-book growth % that NETS OUT deposits/withdrawals (a deposit doesn't inflate it, a withdrawal doesn't read as a loss); distinct from ROI; multi-book aggregation correct; legacy `initial_deposit` migrated; growth hidden until set; honest framing. `uv run pytest` green (backend calc tests). **changelog entry (user-facing).**
‚ö†ÔłŹ SIZE: this is materially bigger than the original card (data model + endpoints + two UI surfaces) ‚ÄĒ if a session finds it too large for one pass, PHASE it: Phase 1 = the data model + per-book balance/deposit/withdrawal + the honest overall growth; Phase 2 = per-book breakdown UI + the opt-in reset. Flag the split in the handoff.
Closeout (per ¬ß0.1): END with an ‚Ź≠ÔłŹ Operator handoff ‚ÄĒ run-order (DynamoDB schema/migration + lambda deploy + the `initial_deposit` migration step), `git add <paths>`, the changelog line, verify-after-deploy (add 2 books, record a deposit + a withdrawal, confirm growth % nets them out correctly).

‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ INC-14 Duplicate `is_current` lineup rows ‚Üí inflated training-sample weight (investigate + fix)   [Model-A / data-correctness ¬∑ ūüĒī OPEN]   (surfaced by E11.1-W1d, 2026-06-25)
WHY: the W1d session downgraded a `unique_combination_of_columns(game_pk, side)` test on `feature_pregame_lineup_features` (error‚Üíwarn) to unblock a merge ‚ÄĒ and it's WARNING, i.e. there ARE duplicate `(game_pk, home_away)` rows. Root-cause hypothesis: `feature_pregame_lineup_state` (SCD-2) has MULTIPLE `is_current=true` rows for the same game+side (the transition failed to flip old rows to `is_current=false`), and `feature_pregame_lineup_features.sql`'s `lineups` CTE (`WHERE is_current=true`) fans them through ‚Üí the feature store ‚Üí **inflated sample weight on affected games in the v6 / E2.x / E5.x training matrices.** The guard is now SOFT so this won't self-surface again. Data-correctness, not a serving outage ‚ÄĒ but it silently biases training.
DO ‚ÄĒ PHASE 1 (QUANTIFY first, don't fix blind):
 ‚ÄĘ Run the diagnostic (Snowflake MCP, read-only): `SELECT game_pk, home_away, COUNT(*) cnt FROM feature_pregame_lineup_state WHERE is_current=true GROUP BY 1,2 HAVING COUNT(*)>1 ORDER BY cnt DESC;` ‚Üí HOW MANY (game√óside) keys are duplicated, over WHAT date range (is it recent / all-history / a specific window?), and the dup multiplicity.
 ‚ÄĘ Trace REACH: do the dupes actually land in `feature_pregame_lineup_features` (and downstream `feature_pregame_game_features` / the training matrix)? Quantify the % of games affected in the train window ‚Üí that's the inflated-weight magnitude. If it's a handful of games ‚Üí minor; if systematic ‚Üí assess whether v6/E2.x/E5.x need a re-fit on de-duped data.

‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E11.7 Pipeline failure-semantics audit + resilience hardening   ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-22.
3-tier contract (HALT/WARN/ALERT-loud) in CLAUDE.md + guide ¬ß0.1 + canonical op‚Üítier map; dbt severity sweep (3 non-serving models ‚Üí warn; serving stays error); full ops/sensor/cron audit = ALL already compliant from the incident fixes (no code change); 12 AST regression guards (test_e11_7_failure_contract.py) prevent INC-3/5/6 recurrence; CI 436 pass / dbtf compile 1762; committed. (Orig spec ‚Üď for reference.)
WHY: a string of incidents shared ONE root ‚ÄĒ the pipeline's halt/warn/skip/alert semantics are inconsistent, so failures either HALT things that shouldn't, SKIP SILENTLY when they should alert, or RUN IN THE WRONG PLACE. INC-3 (sensor_ops ran heavy dbt IN-PROCESS), INC-5 (silent skip on empty DBT_RUNNER_URL), INC-6 (a peripheral player-bio test HALTED the whole pipeline + blocked predictions). Each got a point-fix; this story defines + ENFORCES one contract so it stops being whack-a-mole.
SCOPE BOUNDARY (don't overlap E11.8): E11.7 = the HALT/WARN/SKIP *failure-handling* contract (what a failure DOES). E11.8 = *freshness-alert coverage* (does every feed have a monitor). Complementary ‚ÄĒ E11.7 makes a silent skip ALERT; E11.8 makes every feed WATCHED.

‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E11.9-T2 Convert `feature_pregame_game_features(_raw)` full-CTAS ‚Üí incremental   [Infra ¬∑ cost ¬∑ ‚≠ź biggest remaining Snowflake lever ¬∑ ūüĒí ML-CORRECTNESS-CRITICAL]   (2026-06-23, E11.9 deferral)
WHY: `feature_pregame_game_features(_raw)` is a full `create or replace` of the ENTIRE history on (nearly) every intraday rebuild (~3,233√ó/7d; E11.9-A removed only the *redundant* 2nd rebuild). Converting to `incremental` ‚ÄĒ rebuild only the games whose inputs changed, not all history ‚ÄĒ is the single biggest remaining Snowflake cut. **BUT this mart FEEDS THE LIVE SERVING PATH (predict_today + the serving store), so a stale/incorrect incremental row = bad predictions ‚Üí it was deliberately deferred from E11.9 for validation. Get the SCOPE right or don't ship.**
‚ö†ÔłŹ THE HARD PART ‚ÄĒ the incremental scope (read this twice): a scheduled game's features CHANGE through the day as lineups confirm, weather/odds/probable-pitchers land, EB posteriors update. So "rebuild today's game_pks" is NOT enough ‚ÄĒ you must re-materialize EVERY game whose upstream inputs changed since the last run, or you serve stale features. Safe filter = re-process all games with `game_date >= current_date - N` (N covering late-confirming/retro updates, e.g. 2‚Äď3 days) UNION any game whose source rows updated since the last build (ties to E11.2-T2 `source_status` thinking). Under-scope ‚Üí stale features served (silent, ML-correctness bug). Over-scope ‚Üí less savings but still correct (prefer this if unsure).
Read: feature_pregame_game_features.sql + feature_pregame_game_features_raw.sql (current materialization + the as-of `< game_date` guards from E1.8) + what TRIGGERS the rebuilds (pipeline/ops intraday + lineup rebuild ops) + the freshness gate that reads `_raw` build epoch (predict_today `_FRESHNESS_STALE_HOURS`) + predict_today.py (the live read) + E12 (the tier-aware serving-parity harness ‚ÄĒ REUSE it as the gate) + dbt incremental docs (unique_key, incremental_strategy merge vs delete+insert, on_schema_change).
Do:
 (1) Pick the config: `materialized='incremental'`, `unique_key` = the mart's grain (game_pk, or game_pk+side), `incremental_strategy` = `merge` or `delete+insert`, `on_schema_change='sync_all_columns'`; the `is_incremental()` filter = the SAFE scope above (date window UNION changed-source games). Preserve every E1.8 as-of guard (`< game_date`) ‚ÄĒ incremental must NOT change point-in-time semantics.
 (2) Keep a periodic FULL-REFRESH net (weekly `--full-refresh`, like the daily build) to correct any incremental drift.
 (3) VALIDATE (the gate ‚ÄĒ operator runs the >1-min dbt builds): build incremental and build full-refresh on the SAME data over a multi-day window ‚Üí **assert byte-identical per game √ó per column** (zero diff). Specifically prove NO STALE ROWS: take a game, change an upstream input (lineup/weather), run incremental, confirm that game's features re-materialized. Then run predict_today on both ‚Üí **identical predictions** (E12 harness green, all tiers). 
 (4) Measure the rebuild-cost drop (WAREHOUSE_METERING_HISTORY COMPUTE_WH vs the 57.57 cr/7d E11.9 baseline + the rebuild query count).
Gate/AC: incremental output == full-refresh (byte-identical over the window); proven no-stale-rows on an upstream change; predict_today predictions UNCHANGED (E12 parity green, all tiers); weekly full-refresh net retained; measured credit/rebuild-count reduction; `uv run pytest` + `dbtf compile` green; changelog = none (infra, predictions must NOT change).
Closeout (per ¬ß0.1): the long `dbtf build` validations ‚Üí operator; ‚Ź≠ÔłŹ Operator handoff ‚ÄĒ the incremental-vs-full parity evidence + the no-stale-rows proof + the predict_today parity + the credit delta + git add. ## Epic E13 ‚ÄĒ Liquid-Market Model Re-Evaluation  ūüĒ¨ **(model R&D ¬∑ commissioned 2026-06-21 ¬∑ kill-gated)**

```
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E13.0 home_win/pre forward-validation   ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-21 ‚ÄĒ HOLD-for-deploy.
Pass-2 thin/ambiguous (completed seasons ‚ąí0.0030 Brier, barely over the 0.002 floor; 2026 +0.0017 ‚Čą wash). home_win = confirmed thin-signal target ‚Üí challenger registered, deploy WITHHELD; a 3rd-decimal edge isn't worth bespoke forward infra. The only remaining tiebreaker (live retention on sparse-served features) ‚Üí build GENERIC = E13.5. ūüõĎ POLICY: don't re-run the offline gate ‚ÄĒ periodic re-gates share decisive data ‚Üí noisy ~PROMOTEs that can't advance hysteresis (noted in registry).

ūüĒ¨ VERDICT ‚ÄĒ E13.0 (2026-06-21): **an offline re-run is NOT a valid 2nd hysteresis window. DEPLOY WITHHELD; the 2nd pass must come from FORWARD live-retention, not a re-gate.** Proof (verified against gate code): `evaluate_promotion` computes the entire decision ‚ÄĒ pooled őĒ, paired-bootstrap CI, and the no-season-regression check ‚ÄĒ over `comp_mask = completed_seasons {2024,2025}` ONLY; 2026 is `current_season`, corroboration-only, never in the decision. The 2024/2025 per-game scores are a deterministic function of frozen historical rows (point-in-time-as-of-game; games already played) + fixed seed=42 (glm challenger + xgb/Platt baseline both deterministic). ‚áí **Absent an upstream historical restatement, a `--refresh-cache` re-run reproduces pass-1 BYTE-FOR-BYTE on the decisive folds (2024 őĒ‚ąí0.00378, 2025 őĒ‚ąí0.00387) ‚Üí deterministically PROMOTE again.** Two offline gates 2 days apart are NOT independent windows: they share ~99.6% of decisive data, and the program's own hysteresis design (`promotion_gate.py:32`, `MIN_CONSECUTIVE_PASSES=2`) explicitly demands "a respected re-eval interval ‚Ä¶ to stop monthly redeploys chasing early-season regime noise." Rubber-stamping deploy off a deterministic re-gate would manufacture false hysteresis. The offline verdict is in fact FROZEN at PROMOTE until 2026 itself becomes a completed season (months out). **Pass-1 evidence archived** ‚Üí `gate_v6_vs_v5_home_win_pre_lineup_pass1_2026-06-19.json` (the canonical gate_json filename is variant-derived and WILL be clobbered by any re-run).

  | window | pooled őĒ | CI | 2024 őĒ (n) | 2025 őĒ (n) | 2026 őĒ (n) |
  |---|---|---|---|---|---|

  - **My "byte-identical absent restatement" prediction was FALSIFIED ‚Üí the marts are NOT frozen.** Fresh pull = 10,836‚Üí10,866 rows (+26 new 2026 games, +1 2024 game, +3 training-season). The 2024 fold MOVED: edge nearly **halved** (‚ąí0.0038‚Üí‚ąí0.0021, now barely clears the 0.002 floor on 2024 alone). Mechanism: the **baseline IMPROVED** under backfill (2024 champ Brier 0.2464‚Üí0.2448) while the challenger stayed flat (0.2426‚Üí0.2427) ‚ÄĒ as the arsenal/Stuff+/bullpen backfill fills historical features in, the richer 154-feat xgb closes the gap on the lean 36-feat glm. ‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E13.8 Market-accuracy benchmark: year√óbook line quality (H2H + totals)   [Model-A ¬∑ situational awareness ¬∑ advisory/transparency only]   (2026-06-23, operator)
WHY: before we re-open the MLB totals/H2H markets we need to know WHAT WE'RE TARGETING ‚ÄĒ how accurate the market itself is at setting lines, per bookmaker, per year. That tells us (a) the practical CEILING (the sharpest book's accuracy ‚ÄĒ the bar a "good" model would have to MATCH, since the H2H edge is dead and the product goal is calibration-parity with the close), (b) the SOFT-BOOK SPREAD (where any residual edge could live), and (c) the YEAR TREND (are books sharpening ‚ÄĒ E3.0b already found soft books converging toward Pinnacle). FRAME: advisory/transparency, NOT a +EV claim ‚ÄĒ this is a benchmark report for the operator, not a served feature.
ūüüĘ DON'T REBUILD WHAT EXISTS: `feature_edge_book_market_era_quality.sql` (E3.0b) already computes the core table ‚ÄĒ grain (book, market_type, season) for book ‚ąą {pinnacle,bovada,caesars,fanduel}, market ‚ąą {h2h,totals}, with `closing_brier`, `closing_log_loss`, `mean_vig`, `mean_abs_dist_to_sharp` (vs Pinnacle), all on the leakage-guarded de-vigged CLOSE (snapshot_ts < commence_time). DO ‚ÄĒ Part B (extensions, the new value): (1) WIDEN book coverage beyond the 4 canonical books to the full oddsapi book set in `odds_snapshots_historical` (the mart hard-codes 4 in its `where lower(s.bookmaker) in (...)` ‚ÄĒ generalize it or write a sibling query; keep Pinnacle as the sharp anchor for dist_to_sharp). (3) ADD H2H favorite hit-rate (share of games the de-vigged favorite won) alongside Brier. (4) ANCHOR with REFERENCE ROWS so the numbers are interpretable: the base-rate/no-skill Brier (H2H ‚Čą 0.249 from home-win rate; totals ‚Čą 0.25 from the over rate) and an explicit "Pinnacle = ceiling" callout. Known prior (E13.6): the served market H2H Brier sits ~0.247 (barely beats the 0.249 coin-flip floor) ‚ÄĒ expect H2H books tightly clustered just under no-skill; totals likely carries more separable structure (that's where the open question is).
Leakage/honesty: everything on the CLOSE, every snapshot already < commence_time (preserve that guard); pushes excluded from Brier (already handled), counted separately for the push-rate metric. No column may assert a +EV bet (honest-framing rule) ‚ÄĒ this is a benchmark, not a signal.

‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E13.9 Selective "best-bet" model: abstention + betting-utility objective on the SOFT markets   [Model-A ¬∑ ‚≠ź distinct edge angle ¬∑ market-AWARE exception ¬∑ full LdP discipline]   (2026-06-23, operator)
WHY: every edge test so far graded the model on predicting EVERY game (minimize Brier over all games) or anchored to the line (E13.1). The operator's idea: build a model that DISCRIMINATES on the best bets ‚ÄĒ abstain on most games, fire only on a selected subset, and judge it on that subset's payoff, not all-games accuracy. This is alpha-from-SELECTION (complement to E13.4's alpha-from-features).
ūüĒĎ WHAT MAKES IT DISTINCT FROM THE KILLED E13.1 (read this first ‚ÄĒ do NOT rebuild E13.1): E13.1 trained on all games, anchored to the line, learned the residual ‚Üí dead on CLV. E13.9 is different on TWO axes: (1) the OBJECTIVE is itself selective ‚ÄĒ directly optimize the SELECTED-subset payoff (expected CLV / betting utility) with an explicit ABSTENTION mechanism (the model chooses when NOT to bet), NOT "minimize all-games loss then threshold the output"; (2) it targets the SOFT markets ‚ÄĒ totals-derivatives (team totals / alt totals; data exists in mart_derivative_closes via E2.0) and player props (once E5.1 lands) ‚ÄĒ where E13.8 showed the main line is efficient (Brier ~0.250) but the lazier derivative/alt prices may not be. The MAIN H2H + main totals lines are a NEGATIVE CONTROL only (expect null per E13.8/E13.1).
‚ö†ÔłŹ THE TRAP ‚ÄĒ this framing manufactures fake edges if done naively. "Backtest, keep the games we'd have won, call those best bets" is pure data-mining. GUARDRAILS (non-negotiable, pre-register ALL before any forward look): the selection rule + abstention threshold are PART of the model ‚ÄĒ fit IN-FOLD, validated OUT-OF-FOLD (purged/embargoed CV); the subset size is pre-committed or swept in-fold, NEVER chosen to flatter the result; the verdict is FORWARD/held-out CLV on the SELECTED subset (the cashability gate), with PBO<0.2 + DSR>0 (DSR deflates for the number of configs tried ‚ÄĒ log every config). Market-AWARE is in scope here (explicit exception, like E13.1) ‚ÄĒ judged on beating the close, not accuracy.
ūüĒ¨ BAKE-OFF (per ¬ß0.5): the selective architecture is NOT one design ‚ÄĒ pre-register a CANDIDATE SET of ‚Č•3 selection/abstention approaches and bake them off, Optuna-tuned, judged on forward/held-out CLV on the SELECTED subset under purged CV, PBO<0.2/DSR>0 (the deflation prices in the search). The "e.g." forms below are the candidate set, not a pick-one menu; a single design's miss is NOT a null.
DO: (1) bake off the selective architectures ‚ÄĒ e.g. (a) an expected-value/utility objective over (model fair prob/total vs the book's de-vigged price) with an abstain action, (b) a two-stage "is THIS a bettable edge?" gate trained to predict realized CLV-positivity, (c) a conformal/selective-prediction wrapper over the calibrated model with a tuned abstention threshold ‚ÄĒ each candidate market vs its OWN close (per the E2.6 derivative-gate pattern), each Optuna-tuned, the subset size swept in-fold; (2) run them on totals-derivatives FIRST (E2.0 data ready), props later (post-E5.1); (3) main lines as the negative control; (4) the long CV/forward fits go to the operator. Stratify on is_cold_start (E13.7) where pitcher inputs matter.
MEASUREMENT: this is the consumer that REVIVES E13.5 (generic shadow-serve + forward-CLV harness) ‚ÄĒ stand up E13.5 to shadow-serve the selective policy and accrue forward CLV on the selected subset as games complete. Offline backtest CLV is necessary-not-sufficient; the real verdict is forward.
HONEST EXPECTATION: likely NULL ‚ÄĒ market efficiency is confirmed from E3.1/E4/E1.9/E13.1/E13.8. But it's a genuinely distinct angle and a clean leak-tight null completes the dossier; a soft-market subset hit would be the program's FIRST real betting edge. PRODUCT NOTE (separate from edge): even a null-edge selective layer can power a "highest-conviction / biggest-disagreement picks of the day" surface ‚ÄĒ but framed HONESTLY (higher-variance, "our model's biggest disagreements with the market," NO +EV/beat-the-book claim) unless it clears the CLV gate. Coordinate that surface with E9/honest-framing.
ūüíĺ DATA (per ¬ß0.5): `mart_derivative_closes` (E2.0) is in S3 ‚ÄĒ read via DuckDB; assemble the selection-model feature matrix in ONE pull ‚Üí parquet and run every selective-architecture candidate √ó Optuna trial √ó fold off the cache, never re-query per candidate.
Read: build_roadmap E13.9 row + the E13.1 kill writeup (what NOT to repeat) + E13.8 benchmark (the soft-vs-main-line bar) + E2.6 derivative-gate spec + mart_derivative_closes (E2.0) + betting_ml eval discipline (purged CV / PBO / DSR) + E13.5 prompt (the harness to revive).
Gate/AC: pre-registered selection rule + abstention + subset size; offline selected-subset CLV with PBO<0.2/DSR>0 per market; E13.5 shadow-serve stood up for forward accrual; honest dossier entry (incl. a null). NO +EV product claim without the forward CLV gate. No changelog unless a user-facing surface ships.
Closeout (per ¬ß0.1): long fits ‚Üí operator (run-order, >1-min flagged); ‚Ź≠ÔłŹ handoff = the design doc + ablation_results per market + E13.5 harness + git add. SEQUENCE: after E13.4 (use its winning features) + E5.1 (props); totals-derivatives can start sooner.

The ONLY gap is the PA-grain rollup ‚ÄĒ so this is a small collapse, not a from-scratch build.
DO: a new dbt model, one row per (game_pk, at_bat_number): (1) ENTERING state from the FIRST pitch of the PA (`pitch_number = 1`, or MIN(pitch_number) per at-bat): base_state √ó outs_when_up = the full 24 base-out state (encode as a clean enum), + bat_score_diff / inning / inning_half / count is 0-0 at entry; (2) batter, pitcher, stand/throws handedness (platoon); (3) the PA OUTCOME from the LAST pitch's `plate_appearance_event` (`events`), mapped to a multinomial label {1B,2B,3B,HR,BB,IBB,HBP,K,out,other} + carry `woba_value`/`woba_denom`. Leak-clean: this is a historical record; any serving/eval consumer filters `< game_date`.
BUILD ON THE LAKEHOUSE: `stg_batter_pitches` already reads S3 parquet (read_parquet lakehouse_loc) ‚Üí keep this model on the dbt-duckdb/S3 path, NOT Snowflake (cost posture: profitable-system-first). DuckDB-readable output.

‚Ė∂ INC-16-P5   ‚úÖ EXECUTED LIVE 2026-06-27 (built + deployed + verified end-to-end; all on `main`). ‚Ė∂ INC-16-P5 ‚ÄĒ Orchestration CI/CD in GitHub (gate + auto-deploy future orchestration merges)   [Infra/DevOps ¬∑ ūüß≠ OPUS ¬∑ ‚úÖ UNBLOCKED ‚ÄĒ P4 done (box owns live on `main`) ¬∑ bake-off-EXEMPT]   (2026-06-26, operator)
WHY (the recurring footgun this kills): once the AWS box owns live orchestration, "a pipeline change isn't live until the codeloc redeploys off `main`" is a MANUAL step ‚Üí `main` and the running box silently drift. ‚≠ź **PRIMARY FAILURE MODE P5 EXISTS TO PREVENT (proven repeatedly at P4 cutover): BAKED-IMAGE DRIFT ‚ÄĒ container code is `COPY`'d into the image, so a host `git pull` does NOT update a running container.** Multiple P4 ops ran stale code after a pull until the image was rebuilt. So the CD job's core job is **rebuild AND redeploy the affected images** (`up -d --build <svc>` / `--profile capture build`), never just `git pull`. Compile-only CI already let a runtime break through once (INC-15: W1d wrong-types passed `dbtf compile`, broke `dbt_daily_build` at runtime). And P2/P4 surfaced deploy-only failure modes CI never sees (PEM `\n`-newline; IMDSv2 hop-limit; region-less boto3; **empty-but-present/missing env vars** ‚ÄĒ see env-parity below). This story makes orchestration merges self-gating + self-deploying so neither drift nor those traps recur.
SCOPE = a GitHub Actions workflow triggered on changes to the orchestration paths (`pipeline/**`, `services/dagster/aws/**`, `services/dbt_runner/**`, the capture-Lambda paths, `infrastructure/**`).
TASKS:
1. **CI gate (on PRs touching those paths)** ‚ÄĒ beyond the existing Python fast gate + dbt-Build jobs: (a) **Dagster `dagster definitions validate`** (defs actually LOAD ‚ÄĒ catches import/boot breaks like the observed `_InactiveRpcError` + the INC-15-class runtime break that compile missed); (b) **`docker compose -f services/dagster/aws/docker-compose.yml config`** + a BUILD of the changed images (catches the buildx/AL2023 + Dockerfile breaks); (c) a **lint/assert that the deploy wiring is present** ‚ÄĒ `_normalize_pem` applied wherever `SNOWFLAKE_PRIVATE_KEY` is consumed (resources/__init__.py, write_serving_store.py, dbt_runner entrypoint, every Snowflake-touching capture Lambda), `AWS_DEFAULT_REGION` set in the container/Lambda env, and no reintroduced `DATABASE_URL`/PG reference on serving/capture paths.
1d. **ūüĒĎ ENV-PARITY CHECK (would have caught EVERY P4 env gap pre-deploy).** Maintain a canonical key list (the keys the ops actually read) and assert the box `.env` contains every one ‚ÄĒ non-empty. P4 lost cycles to FOUR missing/empty vars (`ARTIFACTS_FROM_S3`, `CACHE_BUCKET`, `USER_BETS_TABLE`, `USERS_TABLE`) that each failed silently or late (‚ö†ÔłŹ recall: empty-but-present shadows the code default ‚ÄĒ treat `KEY=` as MISSING, not set). The check: grep the ops for `os.environ.get`/`os.environ[` reads ‚Üí diff against the box `.env` (or a committed `env.required` manifest) ‚Üí fail the gate on any missing/empty required key. This + the IAM-grant manifest (the P4 inline policies `credence-s3-api-cache-rw`, `credence-dynamo-user-bets-settle`) should be documented so a fresh box has the full env+IAM set.
2. **CD (on merge to `main`, same paths)** ‚ÄĒ deploy to the box via SSH or SSM Run Command: `git pull` on `main` ‚Üí `docker compose up -d --build` **AND `docker compose --profile capture build`** (the 4 host-cron captures are a separate profile ‚ÄĒ a plain `up --build` won't rebuild them, so capture-entrypoint changes won't take effect) ‚Üí **post-deploy verification**: codeloc defs loaded, daemon up, `dbt-runner /health`={"ok":true}, `head -1 /tmp/snowflake_rsa_key.pem`=`-----BEGIN`, IMDS hop-limit=2 still set. Fail the job loudly (don't leave a half-deploy) if any check fails. Result: `main` == running box automatically ‚ÄĒ the manual codeloc redeploy is GONE.
2a. **Host-cron is NOT reloaded by a git pull.** `capture.crontab` is a tracked file; a change to it requires re-running `crontab capture.crontab` on the box ‚ÄĒ a `git pull` alone does NOT reinstall the host crontab. The CD job must detect a `capture.crontab` change and re-install it (then a no-op otherwise). (Post-P4 the box's copy == committed, so this is clean.)
2b. **Safe-deploy / blue-green (Railway gave us rolling deploys; replace it ‚ÄĒ PHASED).** ‚ö†ÔłŹ Scope note: user-facing SERVING is decoupled from this box (frontend ‚Üí Lambda ‚Üí DynamoDB/S3), so a box redeploy does NOT take the site down ‚ÄĒ what we're protecting is (a) a bad deploy crash-looping a service and (b) killing an in-flight run. Also the Dagster **daemon/scheduler is a singleton** ‚ÄĒ never run two daemons at once (double-run hazard, same as the Dagster+‚ą•box overlap) ‚Üí any blue/green ends in a brief single-owner daemon handoff, not seamless N+1.
   - **NOW (do as part of this story, ~$0):** health-GATED deploy with **auto-rollback** ‚ÄĒ tag/keep the previous image; if the post-deploy checks (step 2) fail, revert to the prior tag instead of leaving it broken. Add a **graceful drain** before recreate: pause the `QueuedRunCoordinator` queue + let in-flight runs finish (or rely on run-retries) so a deploy doesn't sever a live run.
   - **EVENTUAL (defer ‚ÄĒ gated on an uptime SLA, post-beta; do NOT build now):** true blue/green ‚ÄĒ Caddy/ALB-fronted dual stacks for the stateless tier (webserver + code location) with a daemon-ownership handoff, or a standby instance to flip to. Cost ‚Čą a doubled compute footprint during deploys (or a standby box). Flag as a follow-up, not in-scope for the beta.
3. **Secrets/access** ‚ÄĒ use GitHub Actions OIDC ‚Üí an AWS deploy role (no long-lived keys in CI); SSM Run Command preferred over raw SSH (no inbound 22 from GitHub, no key management). ‚õĒ Claude does NOT enter/handle any credential ‚ÄĒ the operator wires the OIDC trust + secrets; the prompt specifies WHAT, the operator provisions.
3a. **Reproducible-box bootstrap (so a fresh box isn't bitten by the P3 gotchas):** fold into cloud-init/provision ‚ÄĒ install + enable cron (`dnf install -y cronie && systemctl enable --now crond`; AL2023 minimal ships NO cron ‚Üí P3 hit `crontab: command not found`), set IMDSv2 hop-limit=2, `AWS_DEFAULT_REGION`, install the `capture.crontab`, and the buildx‚Č•0.17 fix. A rebuilt/replacement box should come up fully wired with zero manual steps. **ūüõ†ÔłŹ ALSO pull in INC-16-P7 task 1 here ‚ÄĒ PIN all compose image tags (kill `:latest`, esp. `flaresolverr:latest`) before wiring auto-`--build`**, else this CD can pull a breaking upstream image onto the live box silently.
4. **Branch protection** ‚ÄĒ require the new CI gate (+ the existing fast gate + dbt jobs) on PRs to `main` for orchestration paths.
CONVENTIONS: do NOT git commit/push (operator); the workflow file lands under `.github/workflows/`; keep it scoped to orchestration paths so app/model PRs aren't slowed.
AC: orchestration-path PRs are CI-gated (defs-validate + compose-build + deploy-wiring asserts, on top of fast gate + dbt jobs); merges to `main` on those paths auto-deploy to the box + self-verify (health + defs + key + IMDS) and **auto-rollback to the prior image on failure** + graceful-drain in-flight runs before recreate; OIDC/SSM access (no static keys, operator-provisioned); branch protection updated; the manual "codeloc redeploy off main" step is eliminated. (True blue/green = a flagged follow-up, not in this story.) Operator handoff with the OIDC/SSM setup steps + the `git add .github/workflows/...` list.

‚Ė∂ INC-16-P6   ‚úÖ EXECUTED LIVE 2026-06-28 (built + deployed via the P5 CD + emails CONFIRMED received). ‚Ė∂ INC-16-P6 ‚ÄĒ Observability + email alerting for the AWS orchestration box   [Infra/SRE ¬∑ ūüß≠ OPUS ¬∑ ‚úÖ DONE ‚ÄĒ was the last INC-16 recovery story ¬∑ bake-off-EXEMPT]   (2026-06-26, operator)
WHY: the box (EC2 `i-07594af1679f81c38`) now runs the live daily cycle + host-cron captures (P5 CI/CD live, schedules ON, Dagster+ OFF) with NO alerting ‚Üí a silent failure (dead box, crashed daemon, failed build, bad deploy) wouldn't surface until someone notices stale picks. ūü™Ě Hook the now-live P5 CD `deploy.sh` verify path too (a failed deploy/auto-rollback should alert). ūüĒ≠ The whole INC-16 build proved serving degrades SILENTLY (P5 even found `SERVING_CACHE_TABLE` empty; P4 found `CACHE_BUCKET` silent-skip) ‚Üí outcome-based alerting is the soak safety net. Add layered observability, **email preferred** (SES is already wired). All ~$0 (CloudWatch alarms ~$0.10/alarm/mo; SNS email + SES effectively free at beta volume). "Dagster goes down" = 3 distinct failure modes ‚Üí one layer each:
TASKS:
1. **ūü™¶ DAILY-OUTPUT DEAD-MAN'S SWITCH (highest value ‚ÄĒ do FIRST; outcome-based, catches ALL root causes).** Alert if today's picks aren't in the DynamoDB serving cache (`credence-prod-serving-cache`) by a cutoff (e.g. 8:00am ET). This fires whether the cause was a dead box, a failed dbt build, a bad deploy, or a stuck daemon ‚ÄĒ it watches the THING USERS SEE, not a process. Implement as a small scheduled check (Lambda+EventBridge, or a CloudWatch metric + "no-data" alarm fed by `write_serving_store` emitting a success metric/heartbeat) ‚Üí SES/SNS email on miss. ‚ö†ÔłŹ Finalize the cutoff + the "today produced" definition once P4 makes the box own the full daily cycle; the check itself can be built now against the current output.
   - ūüĒ¨ **WHY this is THE priority (P4 proved serving degrades SILENTLY):** `write_serving_store` skips ALL S3-fallback writes on a missing `CACHE_BUCKET` (`if bucket:` ‚ÄĒ no error), and WARN-tier settlement swallows errors. Process/health checks would have stayed GREEN while the output silently rotted. Outcome-based alerting (picks present in DynamoDB by cutoff; `mart_odds_outcomes` ingestion_ts advancing) is the ONLY thing that surfaces this class without a human noticing ‚Üí build #1 and the capture-staleness check (#5) FIRST.
2. **ūüďČ BOX / INSTANCE LIVENESS + RESOURCE PRESSURE** ‚ÄĒ CloudWatch **EC2 status-check alarms** (instance + system reachability) ‚Üí SNS topic ‚Üí email subscription (catches instance death / unreachable). Plus resource alarms tuned for this **burstable t4g.medium (2 vCPU, 4 GB, baseline ~40% combined)** ‚ÄĒ calibrated so normal daily-build/predict bursts DON'T page, only genuine trouble:
   - **ūüß† MEMORY/SWAP (highest-value on this box ‚ÄĒ OOM is the likeliest failure, not CPU):** CloudWatch agent `mem_used_percent` > **85%** for 10 min, AND swap-in-use climbing / `swap_used_percent` > ~50% ‚Üí alarm. (The 4 GB box OOM'd heavy PyMC/CatBoost builds before the swapfile; an OOM kills a process outright vs. CPU just slowing.) Pair with a quick `dmesg | grep -i oom` note in the runbook line.
   - **ūüíĹ DISK:** root `disk_used_percent` > **85%** (Docker images/logs/parquet temp fill a small root vol).
   - **ūüĒ• CPU ‚ÄĒ alarm on SUSTAINED, not spikes:** `CPUUtilization` > **90% for 30 min** (3 consecutive 10-min datapoints) ‚Üí investigate. ‚ö†ÔłŹ Do NOT alarm on brief 80‚Äď100% spikes ‚ÄĒ the daily build / `predict_today` / image rebuilds / FanGraphs solves are *expected* minutes-long bursts. The real signal is high CPU **sustained for hours outside a known build window** (baseline is 40%; load average sustained > 2 on the 2 vCPUs = saturated).
   - **ūüéüÔłŹ CPU CREDITS:** if the instance is `standard` mode, alarm `CPUCreditBalance` < **50** (throttle precursor). If `unlimited` (the t4g default ‚ÄĒ confirm via `describe-instance-credit-specifications`), skip the balance alarm and instead watch `CPUSurplusCreditsCharged` trending up (cost, not throttle). At beta volume neither should fire from routine serving; a sustained breach = a runaway process or a heavy retrain mistakenly run on this serving box.
3. **ūüź≥ SERVICE LIVENESS (box up but a container down/daemon not ticking ‚ÄĒ a plain ping misses this)** ‚ÄĒ a host-cron healthcheck (~every 5 min) asserting `docker compose ps` all-Up + `curl` dagit:3000 + dbt-runner:8080/health + flaresolverr:8191; on failure publish to SNS/SES. Optionally also alarm on the Dagster daemon heartbeat going stale (the daemon can be "up" but stop ticking schedules/sensors).
4. **ūüö® DAGSTER RUN-FAILURE ALERTS** ‚ÄĒ wire a Dagster OSS `run_failure_sensor` ‚Üí **SES email**, scoped LOUD to the **HALT-tier** ops (per the CLAUDE.md E11.7 op‚Üítier map: predict_today, dbt_daily_build run-step, write_serving_store, signal_freshness_check, ingest_statcast, the W1 lakehouse ops, ‚Ä¶) so serving-critical failures shout; WARN-tier failures can be digest/suppressed to avoid noise.
5. **‚ôĽÔłŹ REUSE existing signals, don't reinvent** ‚ÄĒ audit `scripts/check_data_freshness.py` + `signal_freshness_check` (already in the repo) and ROUTE their output to the same SES/SNS channel rather than building parallel freshness logic. Note the host-cron captures (P3) too ‚ÄĒ alert if odds capture stops landing in `mart_odds_outcomes` (a capture-specific dead-man switch, since they're host-cron not Dagster-monitored).
6. **Alert hygiene** ‚ÄĒ one SNS topic (or a couple by severity), de-duped/rate-limited so a flapping box doesn't spam; a clear subject convention (`[Credence PROD] ‚Ä¶`); a documented runbook line per alert (what it means + first action). ‚Ė∂ E9.34   ‚úÖ BOTH BUGS FIXED + VERIFIED (Sonnet, 2026-06-28; operator-confirmed post-deploy). 
 ‚ÄĘ **BUG 1 (EV times +5h) ‚ÄĒ RENDER layer:** `stg_statsapi_games.game_date` is TIMESTAMP_TZ ‚Üí Pydantic v2 serializes as `...+00:00` (OFFSET, not `Z`). The prior partial fix's `endsWith("Z")` check missed the offset case ‚Üí appended Z ‚Üí invalid `"...+00:00Z"` ‚Üí browser parsed as LOCAL. Fix: `formatGameTime` now uses the string as-is if it ends in `Z` OR matches `/[+-]\d\d:?\d\d$/`, else appends Z (mirrors game-detail `fmtGameTime`); covers all 3 EV call sites. Dashboard was immune ‚ÄĒ it uses a SERVER-side `game_time_et` (`_format_game_time_et`), never parses `game_start_utc` client-side.
 ‚ÄĘ **BUG 2 (ATL@SF stuck pending) ‚ÄĒ settle filter:** MLB Stats API has TWO terminal codes ‚ÄĒ `'F'` (Final) and `'O'` (Final/Official, after the official scorer; LATE games are usually `'O'` by the nightly settle run). `_final_scores()` in `settle_user_bets.py` queried `status_code = 'F'` only ‚Üí `'O'` games invisible ‚Üí bet stuck pending forever. Fix: `WHERE status_code IN ('F','O')`. TZ hypothesis RULED OUT (settle queries by `game_pk`, not date ‚Üí UTC day boundaries irrelevant).
 Files: `frontend/app/ev-tracker/page.tsx`, `scripts/settle_user_bets.py`, `changelog.json` (2 entries, `2026-06-22` block). CI: tsc + fast gate 683 + changelog-guard green.
 ūüĒĎ DURABLE LESSONS: (a) **Pydantic v2 serializes tz-aware datetimes as `¬Īoffset`, NOT `Z`** ‚Üí any frontend date parsing must handle BOTH (or better, serve a server-side pre-formatted string like Dashboard's `game_time_et` ‚ÄĒ the robust pattern); (b) settle on `('F','O')`, not `'F'` alone. ‚ö†ÔłŹ **PM FOLLOW-UP owed:** the `'F'`-only bug was PRE-EXISTING (not cutover) ‚Üí OTHER late games all season may have bets STILL stuck pending ‚Üí run a one-off re-settle sweep (the fixed job re-queries pending-by-GSI ‚Üí should clear them). (Orig prompt ‚Üď.)
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ E9.34 P1 BUG: EV Tracker game times shifted +5h (one TZ offset) ‚ÄĒ Dashboard is CORRECT   [App ¬∑ ūüĒī P1 TRUST ¬∑ ūüß≠ OPUS ¬∑ frontend + serving ‚ÄĒ diagnose before fixing]   (2026-06-28, operator; screenshot-reported)
WHY (P1 trust): the EV Tracker shows wrong game start times on a BETTING page ‚ÄĒ and the page's own banner tells users "don't bet until confirmed lineups ~90 min before first pitch," so a wrong time can actively mislead a bet. Fix honestly + at the right layer.
ūüĒĎ **THE DIAGNOSTIC LEVER (use this ‚ÄĒ it narrows the search hugely):** the SAME game renders DIFFERENTLY on two pages. MIA @ STL on **Dashboard = `1:15 PM CDT` (CORRECT)**; on **EV Tracker = `6:15 PM CDT` (WRONG)**. őĒ = **+5h = exactly the CDT UTC offset (UTC‚ąí5)** ‚Üí the EV Tracker is doing ONE FEWER UTC‚Üílocal conversion (rendering an 18:15 UTC value as if it were 18:15 local = 6:15 PM). **Because the DASHBOARD is correct, the upstream data is almost certainly FINE** (MLB schedule ‚Üí the W3pre-migrated `stg_statsapi_games` ‚Üí the marts ‚Üí serving) ‚Üí **this is most likely NOT a W3pre/data regression; it's an EV-tracker-specific FIELD or FORMATTER issue.** Don't burn the session chasing the lakehouse.
GROUNDED POINTERS (already inspected):
 ‚ÄĘ EV page render: `frontend/app/ev-tracker/page.tsx` ‚ÄĒ `formatGameTime(isoString)` (~L199) appends `'Z'` to force-UTC-parse a naive timestamp, then `toLocaleTimeString` (browser‚ÜíCDT). Called at ~L268, ~L1279, ~L1348. The field is **`pick.game_start_utc`**; the DATE is a SEPARATE field `pick.game_date` (rendered at `T12:00:00` local). ‚ö†ÔłŹ A `formatGameTime` UTC-fix JUST shipped (W3pre session) yet EV still shows the buggy +5h time ‚Üí either the fix doesn't cover the EV payload's actual string FORMAT (e.g. space-separated `"2026-06-28 18:15:00"` vs `T`-separated ‚Üí `+Z` may not force UTC in the browser), or a render path/value it doesn't reach.
 ‚ÄĘ Dashboard render (the CORRECT one): `frontend/app/page.tsx` ‚ÄĒ find ITS game-time formatter + which field it reads. **DIFF the two: same field? same string format? same formatter logic?** The delta between them IS the bug.
 ‚ÄĘ Serving writer: `scripts/write_serving_store.py` ‚ÄĒ ‚ö†ÔłŹ it aliases **`g.game_date AS game_start_utc`** in some CTEs (~L217, ~L311) BUT also carries a real **`b.game_start_utc`** from `mart_game_odds_bridge` (which derives from `commence_time`) in others (~L254/280/318/336). **So different serving payloads populate `game_start_utc` DIFFERENTLY ‚ÄĒ a real start-timestamp vs a date-at-midnight.** Determine EXACTLY which payload/field the EV-tracker endpoint serves vs what the Dashboard serves; an aliased-`game_date` (midnight) or a `commence_time` with a different format/precision is a prime suspect.
 ‚ÄĘ Backend: `app/backend/routers/picks.py` + `app/backend/models/picks.py` ‚ÄĒ how `game_start_utc` is serialized (does it emit a `Z`/offset, a naive NTZ string, `T`- vs space-separated?). The serialized STRING FORMAT is what makes `formatGameTime`'s `+Z` work or fail.
DEBUG ORDER (reproduce ‚Üí isolate ‚Üí diagnose ‚Üí fix; engineering:debug discipline):
 1. **Capture the raw value at each layer for one game (MIA@STL, 2026-06-28):** the DynamoDB serving payload (`credence-prod-serving-cache`) for BOTH the EV-tracker key AND the dashboard key ‚Üí record the exact `game_start_utc` string each carries (S3 fallback too if relevant).  3. **Diagnose the format:** if both carry `18:15`-ish UTC but EV renders +5h, it's the render (formatGameTime's `+Z` not forcing UTC for that string format) ‚Üí fix the formatter to robustly parse to UTC (normalize `T`/space, ensure a single UTC‚Üílocal conversion; mirror the Dashboard's working formatter). If EV's value is a `game_date`-midnight alias or a differently-typed `commence_time`, fix it at `write_serving_store` (serve the real start timestamp in a consistent UTC ISO format) ‚ÄĒ ‚ö†ÔłŹ serving-write path runs on the AWS box (INC-16) ‚Üí land via the P5 CD, verify post-deploy.
 4. **Pick the RIGHT layer:** prefer normalizing the SERVED format to a single canonical UTC ISO (`...Z`) so every consumer (EV, dashboard, game-detail `picks/[game_pk]` `fmtGameTime`) renders identically ‚ÄĒ then the frontend formatters don't each need their own `+Z` hack.
SECONDARY (note, don't rabbit-hole): the first screenshot shows games tagged "Confirmed" under a "Preliminary predictions ‚ÄĒ lineups not yet confirmed" banner ‚ÄĒ flag whether that's a related state/staleness inconsistency or independent; report, fix only if same root cause.

‚ĒĀ‚ĒĀ‚ĒĀ ADDENDUM (2026-06-28, operator) ‚ÄĒ ūüźě SECOND BUG, likely SAME TZ root cause: a settled game shows UNSETTLED on the Bet Log ‚ĒĀ‚ĒĀ‚ĒĀ
SYMPTOM: an **ATL @ SF** bet is NOT showing as settled on the Bet Log, though the game was **LAST NIGHT**. Investigate WHILE you're in the date/time code ‚ÄĒ there's a strong chance it shares E9.34's UTC-date mishandling.
ūüĒĎ WHY IT MAY BE THE SAME BUG: **ATL @ SF is a Pacific-time (late) game** ‚ÄĒ a ~7pm PT first pitch is **~02:xx UTC the NEXT day**. If any date logic in the settle/results path buckets by **UTC date**, a late West-coast game rolls into the next UTC day ‚Üí it gets mis-dated ‚Üí the settle job looks for its result on the wrong date (or treats it as "not yet played") ‚Üí the bet stays PENDING. That's the exact class of UTC-vs-local error E9.34 is about. **Test this hypothesis first.**
HOW SETTLEMENT WORKS (grounded): bets live in `credence-prod-dynamo-user-bets`; a PENDING bet carries `pending_game_pk` (= game_pk) on the sparse GSI **`gsi-pending-by-game`**; `scripts/settle_user_bets.py` queries that GSI, looks up the game RESULT, writes the outcome, and REMOVEs `pending_game_pk` (that removal = "settled"). The Bet Log `/bets` read surfaces the stored outcome. ‚ö†ÔłŹ `settle_user_bets_op` is **WARN-tier** (CLAUDE.md op‚Üítier map) ‚Üí a failure logs a warning and the op SUCCEEDS ‚Üí SILENT (and P6's `run_failure_alert_sensor` is LOUD only for HALT-tier, so it would NOT have paged).

 1. **Has ANY bet settled since the INC-16 cutover (06-27)?** If NONE ‚Üí the settle job is broken on the new AWS box (systemic), NOT ATL/SF-specific. ‚ö†ÔłŹ P4 Phase-G found `USER_BETS_TABLE` was empty-but-present on the box + added IAM `credence-dynamo-user-bets-settle` ‚ÄĒ verify those are correct AND that the settle op is actually SCHEDULED + RUNNING on the box (check its last run / Dagit). If OTHER bets settled but ATL/SF didn't ‚Üí it's game-specific ‚Üí go to step 2.
 2. **Inspect the ATL/SF bet item** in `credence-prod-dynamo-user-bets`: does it still carry `pending_game_pk`? what `game_pk` / `game_date`? Then check: is that game's **RESULT present** in the results source the settle job reads (`mart_game_results` / wherever `settle_user_bets.py` pulls the final outcome)? If the result is MISSING ‚Üí either the results feed is lagging (note: `mart_odds_events` has been stale since 06-04 ‚ÄĒ a related feed lag is plausible) OR the game_pk/date filter mis-bucketed the late PT game (the TZ hypothesis).

## ūüŹĀ SNOWFLAKE DECOMMISSION PROGRAM ‚ÄĒ E11.1 W4 ‚Üí reader-migration (the "Cortex-only" finish)   [Infra ¬∑ cost ¬∑ ūüß≠ OPUS-ONLY ¬∑ all bake-off-EXEMPT]   (operator 2026-06-28: PUSH straight through, then Opus ‚Üí model work)
**GOAL:** migrate the **35-mart Snowflake residual** (+ the feature/serving READERS) off Snowflake ‚Üí DuckDB/S3. **End-state Snowflake footprint = ONLY the Cortex narrative `generate_pick_narratives.py`.** Drop the July-1 gate (obsolete: P2 put DynamoDB between users & Snowflake ‚Üí marts are read at BATCH time, not request-time).
ūüĆź **ENVIRONMENT REALITY (post-INC-16 ‚ÄĒ READ FIRST; applies to W4/W5/W6/W7):** We are **OFF Railway ENTIRELY** (the workspace was T&S-restricted ‚Üí the plan is CANCELLED ‚ÄĒ there is no Railway). Orchestration = **self-hosted Dagster OSS on AWS EC2** (`i-07594af1679f81c38`); lakehouse builds run THERE via `run_w1_lakehouse_op` ‚ÄĒ **NEVER a "Railway cron."** The serving cache is **DynamoDB `credence-prod-serving-cache`** (P2 deleted the Postgres `api_cache` + `app/backend/services/pg.py` ‚Üí `serving_cache.py`); **there is NO Postgres serving layer and NO `DATABASE_URL`** anywhere; serving read order = **DynamoDB ‚Üí S3**. Cutover ships via the **P5 CD** (merge to `main` auto-deploys OIDC‚ÜíSSM‚Üí`deploy.sh`, rebuilds on `dbt/**`+`scripts/**`; create the `lakehouse_ext` external tables BEFORE the merge). ‚ö†ÔłŹ **Any older prompt/code/comment you read that mentions Railway, a Railway-cron, Railway PG, `DATABASE_URL`, or the PG `api_cache` is STALE ‚ÄĒ do NOT act on it; if you touch that code, strip/flag the stale reference.**
**SHARED MACHINERY (every wave reuses ‚ÄĒ DON'T reinvent; mirror W2/W3-main):** dual-branch model (`{% if target.name=='duckdb' %}` DuckDB transform over S3-views `{% else %}` thin `select * from baseball_data.lakehouse_ext.<model>`; `materialized='view', tags=['wN_lakehouse']`) ¬∑ extend `run_w1_lakehouse.py` (a `W{N}_MART_MODELS` ordered list + `_build_w{N}` that registers each as a view immediately so intra-wave deps resolve) ¬∑ `generate_w{N}_external_tables.py` (mirror the W3 generator; UPPERCASE cols) ¬∑ `refresh_w1_external_tables.py` `W{N}_TABLES` in the HALT/required set ¬∑ a `parity_check_w{N}.py` (game-grain = freshness-aware game_pk no-loss vs current stg; season-grain = row-count tolerance; PK-uniqueness HARD; column-hash WARN; reuse the stg integrity pre-flight).
**DuckDB-compat checklist (each verified, W3-main + W4):** `::number`‚Üí`::decimal(scale)` (explicit scale or values zero); `dateadd('day',n,d)`‚Üí`d + interval 'n days'`; `game_date::date` before any RANGE-window/interval (parquet stores it VARCHAR); a result-cast `(ratio)::numeric` is scale-0 in Snowflake (often DELIBERATELY zeroed) ‚ÄĒ REPRODUCE it, don't "fix" it; confirm every consumer of a zeroed col reads a different (rolling/std) col; **(W4) FanGraphs/big JSON flatten ‚Üí set `threads=2` + a `memory_limit` (else OOM); httpfs ‚Üí raise `http_timeout`; the live `pitcher_clusters` keys on `fit_date` (NOT `snapshot_date`), unique `(pitcher_id, season)`; hash WARNs on FLOAT cols = stringification artifact, not a defect (row-exact + PK-unique is the real gate).** **(W5) `at` is a DuckDB RESERVED word (‚Üí`at_`); a CTE named the SAME as its base table self-references in DuckDB (‚Üírename e.g. `team_ref`); the `{% if is_incremental() %}‚Ä¶{% else %}<real where>{% endif %}` else-arm must be HAND-INLINED (the runner's stripper eats it); a literal `{% else %}` inside a SQL `--` comment BREAKS `dbtf compile` ("unknown statement else"); `dbt_utils.date_spine()` can't survive the extractor ‚Üí inline a DuckDB `range()`; match the retired table's TYPE (`mart_game_results`=DATE, `mart_game_spine`=TIMESTAMP_NTZ ‚ÄĒ cast `game_date::date`/`::timestamp`); incremental‚Üíview = just drop the `incremental` config + the `is_incremental()` WHERE arms (full rebuild). PARITY-PK: pick the TRUE grain ‚ÄĒ `mart_home_away_splits` is per-GAME not per-date ‚Üí PK `(game_pk, team)` (doubleheaders collide on `(team, flag, game_date)`). **(W5b) Snowflake `lateral flatten(input => variant_obj)` ‚Üí DuckDB list-comprehension unnest (`unnest([{...} for k in json_keys(probs)])`); a direct `cast(... as MAP)` on VARCHAR-JSON FAILS. `matched` is a DuckDB reserved word (MERGE). For Bayesian/k-means TOLERANCE-class migrations: seed-pin (`random_state`), the SEEDED cutover is value-exact (parity row-exact-grade); the ~3rd-decimal band only bites on a DuckDB REBUILD ‚Üí parity check both paths (drift bands + MAP-cluster agreement ‚Č•98%).** **ūüßģ BUILDER DUAL-WRITE RULE:** when you migrate a computed-table BUILDER's I/O to `--s3`, that's ADDITIVE if non-migrated consumers (feature layer, deferred marts) still read its Snowflake output ‚Üí KEEP the Snowflake builder run until those consumers migrate; the builder's Snowflake compute is only ELIMINATED once nothing reads its Snowflake table (track this for the cost AC).
**DISCIPLINE (makes fast safe):** per-mart VALUE-PRESERVING parity BEFORE the view swap (this caught 3 latent serving bugs W1d shipped silently); P6 alerting + the P5 CD auto-rollback are the net. ūüö® **GRANT-PRESERVATION (INC-18, 2026-06-29):** every `CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW/TABLE` SILENTLY DROPS Snowflake GRANTs ‚Üí any object on the request-time fallback path (read by `app/backend/routers/picks.py`/`bets.py`) loses `CREDENCE_API_RO`'s SELECT on recreate ‚Üí cache-miss 503. INC-18 added schema FUTURE GRANTS + a staging `+post-hook` re-grant in `dbt_project.yml`; **any wave recreating a request-read object MUST confirm its schema has the FUTURE GRANTS (or a post-hook re-grant)** + verify a Snowflake-fallback request returns 200 post-cutover. **CUTOVER ORDER (P5 CD live):** build S3 parquet ‚Üí `parity GREEN` ‚Üí create the `lakehouse_ext` external tables in Snowflake ‚Üí THEN commit/PR (merge auto-deploys via CD on `dbt/**`+`scripts/**`) ‚Üí verify post-deploy. **A precursor (getting a non-mart Snowflake SOURCE into S3) comes before its marts.**
**SEQUENCING:** the mart GROUPS are independent, but every wave edits the SHARED build scripts (`run_w1_lakehouse.py`/`refresh`/the DDL generator) ‚Üí run **W4‚ÜíW5‚ÜíW6‚ÜíW7 SEQUENTIALLY** (one Opus session each, each builds on the prior's shared-script state) to avoid shared-file merge conflicts. **W7 (readers) is LAST** ‚ÄĒ it needs every mart it consumes already in S3.

GUARDS (serving path): (1) ATOMIC today-partition swap (write-then-register; a failed rewrite leaves the prior good partition live ‚ÄĒ never serve a half-written partition); (2) the partition-aware external table must UNION all partitions (today+history) + the read sees today's partition immediately post-rewrite; (3) parity the FULL table ONCE after the initial partitioned build, then the intraday delta = today's partition only; (4) idempotent today-overwrite each cycle. ūüéĮ **REQUEST-TIME marts are HERE:** the W4 audit put the request-time-FALLBACK reads in this subtree ‚ÄĒ `mart_odds_outcomes`/`mart_game_odds_bridge` are read in the EV/picks/game-detail fallback (P2b fixed `/picks/ev` already).
