‚Ė∂ INC-16-P6a   ‚úÖ DONE 2026-06-28 (committed + pushed `dev` ‚Üí PR‚Üímain‚ÜíP5 CD). **Two-layer suppression:** (1) **deploy-lock** ‚ÄĒ `deploy.sh` writes `/tmp/credence_deploy_in_progress` (after sourcing notify, before any work) + `trap rm EXIT` (clears on success/die/rollback); `healthcheck.sh` SKIPs + resets the fail counter while it exists. (2) **debounce** ‚ÄĒ `/tmp/credence_healthcheck_fail_count` increments per fail, pages only at `FAIL_THRESHOLD=3` consecutive (~15 min), resets to 0 on any success (overridable `HEALTHCHECK_FAIL_THRESHOLD`). Real-outage guard preserved (3 consecutive fails still pages; 1h cooldown prevents spam). ‚ĄĻÔłŹ **Expected one-time blip:** the FIRST deploy of the new `deploy.sh` ran under the OLD (lock-less) deploy.sh ‚Üí one false page ~19:35; all future deploys are protected (unavoidable bootstrap, not a gap). ‚ěē **P2b addendum SHIPPED too:** `write_serving_store.py` now `send_alert`s (via `pipeline/utils/alerting.py`) on DynamoDB failures ‚ÄĒ `_pg_connect` (dedup `dynamodb-connect-failed`) + `_pg_set_cache` put_item (dedup `dynamodb-write-failed`), rate-limited 1/hr, import-guarded no-op outside the container ‚Üí a silent serving-write degradation now PAGES. Files: `healthcheck.sh`, `deploy.sh`, `scripts/write_serving_store.py`. ‚úÖ **Both smoke tests VERIFIED by operator 2026-06-28** (real outage paged `FAIL 1/3‚Üí2/3‚ÜíPAGED`; forced DynamoDB write fail fired the WARNING + SNS) ‚Üí P6a + the P2b write-failure alerting are live-confirmed, no open items. (Orig prompt ‚Üď.)
‚Ė∂ Story prompt ‚ÄĒ INC-16-P6a P6 healthcheck FALSE-POSITIVE ‚ÄĒ "core service(s) down" pages during CD deploys   [Infra/SRE ¬∑ ūüß≠ OPUS (small/contained) ¬∑ P2 alert-hygiene ¬∑ P6 follow-on ¬∑ ships via P5 CD]   (2026-06-28, operator)
WHY: `healthcheck.sh` paged CRITICAL **4√ó in 12h** listing `dagster-codeloc`/`-daemon`/`-webserver`/`dbt-runner` "container down" ‚ÄĒ but the box is healthy (FALSE POSITIVE). Cry-wolf CRITICALs erode trust in the REAL P6 alerts (dead-man switch, the INC-17 model-health alert) ‚Üí fix the noise.
ūü•á **ROOT CAUSE (diagnosed):** the 4 flagged services are EXACTLY the app-image containers the **P5 CD rebuilds** on a `dbt/**`/`scripts/**`/`pipeline/**` merge (`docker compose up -d --build`); `dagster-postgres`/`flaresolverr`/`caddy` (NOT rebuilt) stayed healthy ‚Üí that's why they're absent from the alert. The 5-min host-cron `healthcheck.sh` step-1 check `docker compose ps --status running --services` lands DURING the recreate window ‚Üí those 4 are momentarily `restarting`/`created`, not `running` ‚Üí false "container down". **4 alerts ‚Čą 4 merges/deploys today** (W3pre, W3-main, E9.34, ‚Ä¶), each >1h apart so each clears the 1h cooldown. (NOT the cwd/compose-file gotcha ‚ÄĒ the script already uses the explicit `-f`.)
FIX (combine, in `services/dagster/aws/healthcheck.sh` + `deploy.sh`):
 1. **Debounce ‚ÄĒ require ‚Č•2 (ideally 3) CONSECUTIVE failed checks before paging.** Keep a small counter state file (increment on fail, reset to 0 on success); page only when it crosses the threshold. A transient single-check deploy blip won't page; a REAL sustained outage stays failed across checks ‚Üí still pages (preserve true-positive). This is the robust general fix.
 2. **Deploy-aware suppression:** `deploy.sh` writes a lock (e.g. `/tmp/credence_deploy_in_progress`) at start + removes it in a trap on exit; `healthcheck.sh` SKIPs (or resets the counter, doesn't page) while the lock exists. Directly kills the deploy-window race even if a deploy spans >1 check.
 3. (Optional, sharper liveness) treat `restarting`/`created`/`recreating`/`health: starting` as TRANSIENT (not "down") via `docker inspect` State/Health ‚ÄĒ only `exited`/`dead`/missing = real down. Step-2's `compose exec ‚Ä¶ curl` into codeloc also fails mid-recreate ‚Üí the debounce covers it.
GUARD ‚ÄĒ don't over-suppress: a genuinely-stopped container (`docker compose stop dagster-daemon` left down across ‚Č• threshold checks) MUST still page within ~10‚Äď15 min.
VERIFY: (a) trigger a real CD deploy (or `up -d --build`) ‚Üí confirm NO page; (b) stop a core container and leave it ‚Üí confirm it DOES page after the consecutive-fail threshold; (c) confirm the dead-man switch + other P6 alerts unaffected.
Read: `services/dagster/aws/healthcheck.sh` (the step-1 `ps --status running` + the cooldown), `services/dagster/aws/deploy.sh` (the `up -d --build` window ‚ÄĒ add the lock), `capture.crontab` (the 5-min line).
‚ěē **ALSO (optional, same theme ‚ÄĒ P6 alerting trustworthiness; from P2b 2026-06-28):** `write_serving_store` was found SILENTLY falling to S3-only when its DynamoDB write failed (an IAM gap swallowed as an exception ‚Üí the cache went stale invisibly). Add a LOUD signal: on a DynamoDB write failure, emit a WARNING/alert (via `pipeline/utils/alerting.py`) instead of quietly continuing S3-only ‚ÄĒ so a serving-write degradation pages rather than hides. (Small; fold in if scope allows, else flag as a separate P6 follow-on.)
Gate/AC: no false page during a CD deploy (verified on a real deploy); real sustained outage still pages within ~15 min; debounce + deploy-lock in place; ships via P5 CD; `bash -n` clean. Operator handoff: the change + the verification evidence (a clean deploy with no page + a real-stop that does page).

```
